# Fine Tuning Jobs Operations [#fine-tuning/jobs]

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs [#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs]

_Get Fine Tuning Jobs_

Get a list of fine-tuning jobs for your organization and user.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs [#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job]

_Create Fine Tuning Job_

Create a new fine-tuning job, it will be queued for processing.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/start [#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job]

_Start Fine Tuning Job_

Request the start of a validated fine tuning job.

<Section variant="top-level">
